The nose behind this fragrance is François Demachy. Top notes are Calabrian bergamot and Pepper; middle notes are Sichuan Pepper, Lavender, Pink Pepper, Vetiver, Patchouli, Geranium and elemi; base notes are Ambroxan, Cedar and Labdanum. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Dior launches its new fragrance Sauvage, with the name originating from the fragrance Eau Sauvage from 1966, although the two don’t belong to the same collection. Sauvage is inspired by wild, open spaces; blue sky that covers rocky landscapes, hot under the desert sun.</p>

<p>Dior in-house perfumer, François Demachy, signed this creation. The fragrance is announced as radically fresh, raw and noble at the same time. The composition is reportedly prevalent with carefully selected natural ingredients. Fresh top notes of Calabria bergamot encounter ambroxan, obtained from precious ambergris, and its woody trail.</p>

<p>Dior Sauvage comes out in September 2015, advertised by actor Johnny Depp. It is available as 60 and 100 ml Eau de Toilette.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2145312">sea.chicken</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-21"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1729575306" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Smells identical to JPG Le Male Elixir 😻😍😍😍</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2323428"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2323428#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2323070" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2323070" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="local7"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1547197"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1547197.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="local7" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2323070ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2323070" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1547197">local7</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-21"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1729545324" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have a bottle with batch code from December 2022. It has about 6-8 hours or more longevity and fantastic projection. I don't understand how anyone would be disappointed in it.<br />
<br />
Because there is so much bellyaching about reformulation in 2018 and possibly later, I spent three hours on Ebay last week looking for the oldest batch I could find. The oldest advertised was 2016. I literally looked at every batch code I could find. I finally found a tester posted by someone who had no idea its age (advertised it as "new" tester). It had batch code 5T01 -- first week of June 2015. It was 100% full. I bought it for $75.<br />
<br />
I got it in today. There are no significant differences in projection or longevity with my 2022 batch. The only real difference is that the 2022 batch has a sharper citrus opening (a good thing) and I think smells better and is possibly STRONGER than the 2015 batch. I read one review which talks about the old batches having a sort of "sweaty note" on the dry down which I can maybe faintly tell ... and I see no real advantage to it. I've seen another review where they say there is about a 5% difference in smell and an hour less in longevity. Again, I see no difference in longevity and whatever differences they may be in smell (e.g. "sweaty") are completely insignificant.<br />
<br />
If that's not enough, go look at the YouTube reviews for Sauvage at its launch in 2015 -- like  Redolessence who said "As far as the longevity goes, I do think it's a little bit above average. It is an eau de toilette concentration. I typically get like 6 to 7 hours, and as far as projection goes, I think it's in the average range. I get about an hour or two of projection and I think that's mainly because of the volatility of the bergamot note, and then it starts to sit a little bit closer to the skin. Maybe I get like 5 or 6 hours total from projection from this scent. As far as versatility goes, the versatility is excellent."<br />
<br />
He then goes on to describe the incredible number of compliments he got from it. I am getting all this and better with my 2022 batch.<br />
<br />
So this reformulation myth about Sauvage being weaker or worse needs to die. It's every bit as good now if not BETTER than it was then. There is NO SIGNIFICANT DIFFERENCE in projection, longevity or overall quality of the scent. I am not a Dior shill. I am just honest. If you get a bottle of it today, you are getting what's always been.<br />
<br />
Sauvage is an intentionally simple, mass-appealing frag that smells fabulous. Even with its popularity, the average person has no clue what it is and it is therefore just as enjoyable and interesting today as it was in 2015.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
some years later people hated sauvage. was it the smell? was it me? was it their ex? now I'm left with disappointment and 30ml left of this thing. was it good when i used it?<br />
<br />
yeah, the people who smelled it on me, myself included, loved it. and I personally liked it because of its versatility.<br />
<br />
will i use it ever again? no. i can't even wear it anywhere as everybody will recognize it and be repulsed because its sauvage. not even particularly the smell.<br />
<br />
im not sure how it came to be this way. but the way i view sauvage now has also changed. i used to like it. now, its just sauvage. and it smells like sauvage. and its probably going to sit in my closet for a long time before its empty.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2321314" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Deesea66"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2289360"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Deesea66" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2321314ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2321314" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2289360">Deesea66</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-19">10/19/24 19:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I get a rugged/rakish vibe from this scent.  <br />
<br />
Masculine blast of bergamot and pepper that really screams out and wants to be heard! Then I sense the lavender and patchouli which taste a bit flamboyant, and feminine.  I get stuck on that mix and can't easily classify it as bold and fresh or obnoxious and stinky...  Is it a mysterious smell?  Is it an overly confident smell?<br />
<br />
A deeper, closer smell and I get a sticky, gooey, tree resiny scent that I have to get in and search for.  When I find it, it's nasty, unapologetic, and hard not to notice.  <br />
<br />
It smells and feels a way that matches the advertisements closely.  The color of the bottle, the style of the photo shoots, Johnny Depp's clothing style.  That's exactly what it is.<br />
<br />
I really like this one and can understand why some might say its a scent to wear ironically.  It does give Johnny Depp vibes and it would be quite embarrassing to find yourself smelling like this at the office or a chill dinner with close friends.  It could be the kind of scent you would wear around strangers, if you know what I mean.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2321314"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2321314#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2320719" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2319589" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="EauDeSparta"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2290486"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2290486.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="EauDeSparta" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2319589ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2319589" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2290486">EauDeSparta</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-18">10/18/24 05:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It is truly an impressive fragrance for me. It starts with an energetic opening of bergamot and pepper; the freshness I feel when I first spray it immediately grabs my attention. Its longevity is great, and the projection is quite good too; I receive positive feedback from those around me throughout the day. It works well in every season and for any occasion, making it a versatile choice. The bottle design is also very stylish and eye-catching. However, the intense composition of ambroxan and spicy notes can be overwhelming for some. Additionally, due to its popularity, I feel that many people use it, which can be an issue for those seeking something more unique. 7.8/10<br />
<br />
Dior Sauvage EDT, benim için gerçekten etkileyici bir parfüm. Bergamot ve biber notalarıyla enerjik bir açılış yapıyor; ilk sıkıldığında duyduğum ferahlık hemen dikkatimi çekiyor. Kalıcılığı harika ve yayılımı da oldukça iyi; gün boyunca etrafımdaki insanlardan olumlu geri dönüşler alıyorum. Yılın her zamanı ve her ortama uyum sağlayabiliyor, bu da onu çok yönlü bir seçenek haline getiriyor. Şişe tasarımı da oldukça şık ve dikkat çekici. Ancak, ambroxan ve baharatlı notalarının yoğun yapısı bazılarına fazla gelebilir. Ayrıca, popülaritesi nedeniyle çok sayıda insan tarafından kullanıldığını hissediyorum, bu da özgünlük arayanlar için sorun olabilir. 7.8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The scent is not too complicated, it smells clean, fresh, civilized.<br />
The bottle reminds me of a skyscraper at night, and I also think the perfume smells like that too, like nightlife, a night walk in a big city's center surrounded by crispy night's air, the peak of modern present civilization.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1410791">BASMAJ</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-01">10/01/24 12:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I never cared about others' opinions on how common or overhyped Sauvage fragrances are, but are they overpriced?  Yes, I agree on that part... Many would also agree that this DNA needs time to be appreciated more and more...<br />
<br />
The EDP has a warmer, spicier, bright opening, and the late dry-down has smooth amber added... I love it, but I love the EDT more for its simplicity and because it’s very nostalgic for me... It has more of the smell of holy basil that I used to rub my hands with since childhood... I know there is no basil in the blend of the EDT, but I swear it’s identical to holy basil, or Ocimum sanctum, also known as Tulsi 💚🌿 (I googled it )... It is a well-known and widespread type of basil, often grown in homes by the gate for decoration... It has small flowers that look somewhat like lavender, but the flowers are white and purple in color.... the smell of it in this DNA but more prominent in the EDT &amp; I love it!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2185321">AJ Amit</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-28">09/28/24 00:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Its a wild bergamote with full of freshness, sharp, peppery, metalic, citrusy with touch of lavender and covered with beast mode of ambroxan. Its highly versatile fragrance can be wear anytime and anywhere.<br />
<br />
The longevity is 7-8 hour with 4-5 sprays with beast projection for first 3 hours. It is a really masterpiece in blue fragrance IMO and its dry down is really feels awesome.This is the first perfume i have ever been used which is much last longer than others even though its EDT version.<br />
<br />
I have also used Sauavge EDP which is darker and smoother than EDT and one of the best in sauvage line. But original is the masterpiece ever.<br />
  <br />
Sauvage EDT rating:<br />
Scent - 10/10<br />
Longevity - 9/10 (7-8 hour)<br />
Projection - 9/10 (3 hour)<br />
Price - 6/10 ( bit higher based on performance)<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2224902">FoxHound215</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-07">09/07/24 11:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After I used a bit and some oxygen got into the bottle, I can finally detect the citrus in this one, but it isn’t apparent. If you haven’t smelled this one, it’s very distinct. A friend walked past me wearing it and I was able to call it out right away. It’s strong and it punches you in the face and it has a bit of a chemical / artificial scent to it. You know how you drink sprite and you can taste/ feel the carbonated bubbles as it goes down? That’s what smelling this is like. If you can take a scent and carbonate it, that’s what you get with Dior Sauvage. I think it’s okay, but my wife loves it. Anytime I wear it, she says, “oh wow that smells good, what are you wearing?” Lots of people like it, but I once received the opposite of a compliment when someone said it smelled like a doctors office.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2213492">Scheherazade_x</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-04">09/04/24 02:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Day 2 of my Sauvage trial, and it’s on to the EDT. Much like the EDP, the initial spray is heavy on the bergamot, but here it appears a little lighter and fresher (perhaps because the concentration is lower). Then comes a hit of warm, spicy heat from the Sichuan pepper. As it settles, the lavender becomes more prominent. So far, so familiar. <br />
<br />
This one starts to differ in that, to my nose anyway, it’s undertone is less immediately mineral/marine and a bit more woody/earthy - probably thanks to the cedar, vetiver, and patchouli. It’s also slightly less sweet than the EDP, as it doesn’t have the vanilla. <br />
<br />
The EDT definitely feels less “dense” than the EDP, and (being less sweet) is more characteristically “masculine”. Overall a very clean “blue” fragrance that would be well suited to warmer days, but could easily be worn any time of year.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2270950"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2270950#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2268899" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2230006">Jetpack</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-31">08/31/24 09:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Sauvage Eau de Toilette by Dior is a François Demachy masterpiece, embodying the signature and DNA of Dior in a fresh and modern fragrance. Launched in 2015, this scent has quickly become a classic in the world of men's fragrances, known for its versatility and timeless appeal.<br />
<br />
The fragrance opens with a bright and invigorating burst of Calabrian bergamot, paired with spicy Sichuan pepper, creating a fresh and dynamic start. As it develops, aromatic notes of lavender and geranium add a clean, herbal touch, while the base of ambroxan, cedar, and vetiver provides a smoky, woody depth that enhances its longevity.<br />
<br />
Sauvage Eau de Toilette is a good, classic, and universal men's scent, perfect for any occasion. Its balance of fresh and woody notes makes it a versatile choice, whether for everyday wear or special occasions, capturing the essence of modern masculinity with the refined touch of Dior.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1523900">Rynal1511</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-31">08/31/24 02:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance brings back so much memories to me in a positive way. <br />
<br />
While working night shift at my previous job in 2016 I remember one of my mates talking about this fragrance and the hype around it. At the time everyone was talking about it and I started to get into fragrance all because of the Sauvage hype. Unfortunately I didn't get to purchase a full bottle a year later due to the price but it was probably the best decision of my life! Compliments after compliments! <br />
<br />
The projection, the longevity, the scent profile at the time was like no other. Heck I even remember over spraying and going to a restaurant and choking out my family from the scent. Ahh good memories. This one was one of the second bottles I remember finishing so I decided to purchase another full bottle.<br />
<br />
Quite frankly I don't understand why this fragrance gets so much hate but probably from TikTok and the younger generation. Back when this first came out it was a beast and still is although I don't wear it as much as I used to and that's primarily due to owning over 130+ fragrances.<br />
<br />
It you want an all rounder versatile beast, this is the fragrance for you. Don't listen to the haters and I strongly urge you to test it yourself but be warned it is called the 'you smell like my ex' fragrance for a reason.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Regardless of what 'fragheads' say, and I consider myself one with over 150 bottles, this is objectively a fantastic smelling scent that performs great. <br />
<br />
My biggest issue with it is Luna Rossa Carbon. Smells basically the same as Sauvage but is smoother/rounder/more gentlemany so it makes owning both redundant. <br />
<br />
If the Prada didn't exist this would be one of the fragrances I wear the most. Fresh, metallic, spicy, lavender gives it a nice clean touch ... great fragrance and it's popular for a reason.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2252043"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2252043#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2251669" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2250923" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SenselessReviews"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1307154"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1307154.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="SenselessReviews" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2250923ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x0"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2250923" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1307154">SenselessReviews</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-16">08/16/24 00:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I made my film debut as "Random Whore #1" in the 1998 blockbuster "Lethal Weapon 4." I shared the screen with  Danny Glover, the towering straight cop to Mel Gibson's wild cop.<br />
<br />
Danny was a perfectionist. The way he incredulously growled, "Why are there scabs there?!" during our strip search scene is a high-water mark in cinema. Off-camera, we were friendly enough that he showed me exactly where his Sailor Moon tattoo is (the rumors are true).<br />
<br />
One day, after filming wrapped, I invited Danny to lunch at Wendy's. He crunched into a bacon-heavy monstrosity, orange goo dripping down his cheeks. He was about to say something when his eyes widened.<br />
<br />
"What's wrong?" I asked.<br />
<br />
"My burger... It's..."<br />
<br />
Danny covered his mouth and cringed. He leapt from his seat and ran to the lobby.<br />
<br />
"Get out of the damn way!" he yelled, sending Girl Scouts scattering like mice<br />
<br />
"I'm too old for this sh-t!" he wailed, rotating his backside toward a cardboard cutout of Dave Thomas, the kindly Wendy's founder.<br />
<br />
A loud clapping noise reverberated throughout Wendy's. Danny disappeared in a cloud of debris. I darted towards him.<br />
<br />
"Awwwwwww," Danny moaned, still hidden.<br />
<br />
As the cloud dissipated, Danny was curled up in the fetal position. Raw bum cheeks protruded from a tattered opening in his pants. Dave Thomas's smiling face was now smoldering cardboard.<br />
<br />
I was in such shock that I barely noticed my nostril hairs contorting. The smell. Unbearable. A cross between rotting fruit and your hyper cousin force-burping the alphabet.<br />
<br />
Yet it still smelled better than "Dior Sauvage."</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2250923"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2250923#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2250495" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Its intended to be a metallic shower gel mass appealing fragrance, the top notes opening got me and evidently many others since I smell this profile everywhere. For me and my skin however, once this settles gives off an old man type vibe (I'm in my 30s) that was noticed by my wife which I disagreed with until a couple random interactions with strangers said the same thing. It probably is the peppers with the vetiver that really pop off my skin in particular, the ambroxan probably doesn't help in that regard as it projects that out and maybe left me nose blind. Performance is good, lasts 7-10 hours and projects deceptively well. This is the perfume my husband likes and uses the most, and honestly, the one I love the most on him as well (and he has/had quite some good, well-ranked fragrances). <br />
<br />
None of my male friends, relatives, or colleagues use Sauvage. And I never smell it in a public place either. So why are people saying it's overused?<br />
<br />
After all the designer and niche perfumes I smelled, tested, sampled, and bought, I still love Sauvage and think it smells amazing - in the bottle, on my husband's skin, on his clothes, and during every season or time of day. <br />
<br />
I think people should start choosing their perfume based on how it makes them feel and how they perceive it and stop looking at what other "connaisseurs" are saying.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2137868">EmilZakaryan924</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-25">07/25/24 20:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The freshest Sauvage out of the flankers, not as versatile as the EDP, not as spicy and dark as the Parfum and Elixir, but still a nice scent, although it is very popular and used by many. Starts off very ambroxan heavy, citrusy and fresh spicy. <br />
<br />
Lets talk about performance. I get around 6-7 hours with a medium-loud projection leaning masculine. This is versatile like the EDP, I suggest this for spring, summer, fall and maybe the winter. You can wear this in the day and night in my personal opinion. <br />
<br />
Lastly, is it a safe blind buy? Definitely. If you love blue fragrances, this is for you. <br />
<br />
In conclusion: <br />
Scent: 8.5/10<br />
Longevity: 8/10<br />
Projection: 7/10<br />
Versatility: 9/10<br />
<br />
Dior Sauvage Eau de Toilette: 9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2229592"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2229592#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2229467" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1370156">Afc_Croatian</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-02">07/02/24 08:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I will be honest, when I first purchased this I thought it was one of the best things ever.<br />
Then I grew my collection and it became less of a daily-wear for me, more of a gym scent &amp; something I wear around my gf since she loves it on me.<br />
<br />
When a fragrance becomes popular, it's like a double-edged sword, because no matter what you say about it and who wears it, is technically true. You can describe any man wearing this and it's true since almost every demographic of individual has worn this. <br />
<br />
That being said, I beg of you to please refrain from the harsh reviews below and just try it for yourself, if you have just begun your fragrance journey, this is a fantastic first scent to own: it's long-lasting, a compliment-puller &amp; pretty easy to wear. Everyone will have an opinion on this, good or bad, but believe me when I say that 99% of people don't wear scents daily or religiously like you &amp; I do.<br />
<br />
Also, Sauvage is nowhere near as popular as a few years ago, Le Male Elixir &amp; Stronger With You's line is seen on every other tiktok &amp; social media video. Good, let those be popular, Le Male Elixir is a tough sweet wear and SWYI's scent isn't that unique. At least Sauvage is more mass-appealing than both and has a better scent profile IMO.<br />
<br />
Sauvage's opening is a smooth pepper with bergamot lingering around for a few hours but that pepper stays dominant all throughout the profile. If that is not your vibe then I understand, but wow does it ever attract attention.<br />
<br />
120 scents later and to me this is still a 9/10. Some people make accounts on Fragrantica just to bash some beloved scents, make your own opinions and try it for yourself. (IMO Sauvage parfum is the best)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2205769"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2205769#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2204468" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1995052">sIzzled</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-10">06/10/24 20:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>ngas gonna hate but ts gas</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2184461"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2184461#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2184333" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2184333" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="bunn100"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2129907"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2129907.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="bunn100" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2184333ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2184333" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2129907">bunn100</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-10">06/10/24 18:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The fragrance that seems to be as ubiquitous as that one friend who still quotes "Anchorman" in 2024. Sauvage quickly rose to fame, fueled by rugged advertising and the charisma of Johnny Depp. But does it still grab attention like a VIP guest, or has it become the scent equivalent of sending a friend request on MySpace?<br />
<br />
Scent Profile<br />
The fragrance opens with a blast of bergamot and pepper. Imagine you’ve just walked into a citrus grove with a pepper grinder in hand. It’s fresh, spicy, and makes quite the first impression—like someone who high-fives too hard. You’ll think, “Wow, this is bold!” until you realize you’ve smelled this exact combination on every third guy in line for coffee.<br />
<br />
As the initial zest fades, you’re left with a heart of Sichuan pepper, lavender, pink pepper, vetiver, patchouli, and geranium. It’s a spicy, floral, woody mix that’s pleasant but familiar. It’s like the dependable friend who always brings the same dish to potlucks—it’s good, but you’ve had it a million times. The vetiver tries to add some sophistication, but it’s like putting a monocle on a raccoon—it’s still a raccoon.<br />
<br />
The dry down features ambroxan, cedar, labdanum, and elemi. Picture yourself in a woodshop that’s also selling candles and herbal tea. It’s warm, woody, and a bit resinous, creating a dry down that’s quite appealing. But again, it’s nothing you haven’t encountered before on a crowded Saturday night out.<br />
<br />
Longevity and Sillage<br />
Here’s where Dior Sauvage still manages to shine—it’s like the Energizer Bunny of fragrances. Expect it to last a good 8-10 hours, lingering like that one guest who doesn’t know when to leave. The sillage is strong too; you’ll leave a scent trail that could lead a search party right to you. So, if you want to be remembered—or at least not forgotten quickly—Sauvage has got your back.<br />
<br />
Versatility<br />
Wear it anywhere, and it’ll fit right in. Perfect for work, dates, and casual outings, it’s the fragrance equivalent of saying “safe choice.” But therein lies the problem: it’s so versatile and popular that it’s become the Starbucks Pumpkin Spice Latte of colognes. Good? Yes. Unique? Not anymore.<br />
<br />
Overall Impressions<br />
Christian Dior Sauvage is for the guy who wants to smell good without taking any risks. It’s like showing up to a party in a tuxedo T-shirt—stylish but predictable. It’s undeniably pleasant, but if you’re looking to stand out, this might not be your ticket to fragrance fame.<br />
<br />
In conclusion, Christian Dior Sauvage is like a blockbuster movie everyone’s seen. It’s reliable, enjoyable, and has mass appeal, but it won’t make you the star of the show. So spritz it on if you want to play it safe and smell great, but don’t expect to be the only one wearing it in a room full of cologne connoisseurs. Just remember, sometimes standing out means taking a step away from the crowd—unless, of course, you’re fine with being Sauvage-ly standard.<br />
<br />
Sniff-O-Meter Score<br />
<br />
Scent Appeal: 4 - Fresh and spicy, like a splash of cold water on a hot day. It’s crisp and invigorating.”<br />
Longevity: 5 - “Lasts well through the day, with good staying power that keeps you smelling fresh.”<br />
Sillage: 4 - Creates a noticeable and strong presence.”<br />
Uniqueness: 2 - “Popular, enough said.”<br />
Versatility: 4 - “Suitable for a variety of occasions, from casual to formal, though it might not shine in extremely cold weather.”<br />
<br />
Overall Sniff-O-Meter Score: 19/25</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2184333"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2184333#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2184303" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
If you're in the UK and you're not wearing a tracksuit, fake gold chains &amp; a pair of Air Max's then this fragrance kind of feels out of place. Every 18 year old going to his first club night was drowned in this with the hope of taking home whichever woman was intoxicated by Sauvage (and copious amounts of vodka). And rightly so. This fragrance smells incredible, longevity is insane and the Sillage fills a room in nanoseconds. Just a shame that such unsavoury characters gripped onto this scent and ran it into the ground. Can't smell this without the thought of remnant weed clouds and shouting at passers by next to the corner shop while you choke out your pitbull on its chain as it foams at the mouth. <br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2174877" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="accursednholy"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2039413"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2039413.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="accursednholy" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Valentino/Valentino-Uomo-Born-in-Roma-55963.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.55963.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Valentino Uomo Born in Roma"title="Valentino Uomo Born in Roma"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2174877ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2174877" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2039413">accursednholy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-01">06/01/24 15:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After using this fragrance for over a month, asking 20+ people for their opinions, I want to update my review. <br />
<br />
THIS IS AMAZING. I am currently unable to understand how people find this fragrance stale or uninteresting. I asked many people for their opinions without telling them what it is, 3 out of 10 people said "Yeah I know this smell" and one of those people said "My dad wears this it smells SO GOOD", the others couldn't name the fragrance but said it smells almost perfect.<br />
<br />
One time, in Drama class, teacher was complaining about a strong "onion" smell being present in class because of the fair outside, but, and I quote, "At least someone has a perfume so good that it masks the onion smell." I was sitting 2 meters away from him and no one else had a fragrance on.<br />
<br />
I received almost as many compliments that I received when I wore Ultra Male.<br />
<br />
Performance is superb, longevity is good and the smell is near perfect, people keep saying it smells synthetic and low quality but I genuinely think they are delusional lol. Ambroxan does smell screechy, it is what is it, doesn't mean it smells low quality. <br />
<br />
No one can go wrong with Sauvage. Wear it. This is a masterpiece with lots of haters around.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2174877"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2174877#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2174800" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2174800" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Smirky"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1937759"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1937759.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Smirky" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Alexandria-Fragrances/Dapper-1959-61624.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.61624.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Dapper 1959"title="Dapper 1959"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2174800ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2174800" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1937759">Smirky</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-01">06/01/24 13:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a combined review of Sauvage EDT, EDP and Parfum after having tested all three on consecutive days. The Sauvage line, in general, is very popular for a reason. These are excellent, masculine fragrances that are very versatile, working any time of the day, any day of the year, hot or cold or in between. They are also very people pleasing in that most who smell these perfumes on a guy will say they are pleasant scents and attractive. Thus, they are all an easy grab for most situations. They also work for most men of any age. Dior quality is evident in all three perfumes.<br />
<br />
There is a concern about the popularity and not standing out with them or being unique. I can't address that aspect because I live in a rural area where the vast majority of men do not wear any fragrance at all. So, no problem for me.<br />
<br />
Regarding how different the three perfumes are from each other, I'd say the Sauvage DNA is quite clearly shared in the EDT, EDP and Parfum. Elixir (which I reviewed a few months back and revisited as a comparision) goes a little more afield. As an analogy, I'd say the EDT, EDP and Parfum are like brothers while the Elixir is a cousin. Still, the EDT, EDP and Parfum are sufficiently unique that it isn't redundant to own all three if you like the different aspects of each.<br />
<br />
To sum up these aspects, the EDT is more citrusy, the EDP is smoother, rounder and creamier than the EDT while the Parfum is a more woody version of the EDP. The Elixir is a more warm spicy fragrance with touches of cinnamon and licorice.<br />
<br />
If a guy is unsure about which to get, I highly recommend purchasing samples of all four and wearing each on separate consecutive days. That's what I did. This is a much better approach than sniffing all four on test strips in a store. My personal choice is to go with the EDP and the Elixir as I do not have a goal to own all four just for the sake of a complete collection. Of course this is subjective, but the EDP and the Elixir were the most appealing to me.<br />
<br />
Performance of the EDT, EDP and Parfume are all quite good with the EDP having the best performance for me. (The Elixir is in a class by itself - a truly beast mode fragrance that requires experimentation to determine the quantity to apply. It can easily become overwhelming if too much is applied.)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2174800"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2174800#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2174561" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I don't need to say anything else about this fragrance because it has been said a million times before.<br />
7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2174561"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2174561#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2174433" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1390483">Aslanyus</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-30">05/30/24 12:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Hi, everyone I'm going to share my thoughts on Dior Sauvage EDT. It smells very clean and airy it has spicy edge with high dose of ambroxan which makes it very unique, but at the same time it is most purchased men's fragrance, which is bad thing for many fragrances enthusiasts including me. I can't say I'm big fan of sauvage and I can't say it's a bad fragrance it's a perfect fragrance for average customer it has high compliment factor it's clean, fresh and long lasting everything you would want from a mainstream fragrance. My objective overall rating for Dior sauvage is 8/10<br />
thanks guys if you gave your time to read my thoughts about this fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2172633"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2172633#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2172127" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; What a guy 😂</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2162827"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2162827#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2162679" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2162679" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="colognexxx"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108015"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2108015.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="colognexxx" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Saffron-Lazuli-59562.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.59562.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Saffron Lazuli"title="Saffron Lazuli"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2162679ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2162679" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108015">colognexxx</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-20">05/20/24 21:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Dior Sauvage, once a beloved staple in the world of men's fragrances, now feels dated and uninspiring. Over time, it has undergone reformulations that have significantly impacted its longevity and projection. What was once a robust and long-lasting scent now fades much quicker, losing its initial allure.<br />
<br />
Wearing Dior Sauvage today does little to set you apart; its ubiquity makes it a common choice, leading to a lack of uniqueness. When seeking opinions, the response is often lukewarm—typically a polite, "Yes, it's nice," rather than genuine enthusiasm. This cologne has become mundane, blending into the sea of generic scents.<br />
<br />
In a market where individuality and distinctiveness are highly valued, Dior Sauvage falls short. It no longer captivates or stands out, rendering it a rather boring choice for modern fragrance enthusiasts.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2162679"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2162679#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2161908" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Finally smelled it a while back, it's not even that bad, people are exaggerating how it "assaults" or "attacks" their noses. It's sharp, sure, but stop overreacting. It's fresh, peppery, and citrusy, which makes it versatile for mostly any setting. Not to mention this is probably the longest-lasting blue fragrance of all time. I sprayed it on my wrist and I could still smell it clearly 8 hours later. Dior has the best atomizers in the fragrance world as well, so spraying this is a very smooth process. It suffers because the fboy stereotype has brought down its reputation. And yes, most cologne users will probably own this, but it's because it's one of the most mass-appealing fragrances of all time. Dior is rolling in the dough because of this fragrance. Overall, I won't buy because I prefer the elixir concentration of Sauvage, but it's a great beginner fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="2161870"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=2161870#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="31861" sentiment="all"></reviews-infinity>

Dior still has a wide range of beautiful creations that are available in most department stores and online retailers.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="640564"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=640564#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1571838" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
