padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1508898">TjSmellsGood</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-26">05/26/22 20:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm surprised to see so many loving comments of Sauvage on here, not because it's bad but because it's become popular to hate it. I remember before it became super popular as the go-to scent, everyone loved it. Suddenly now that it's popular you'll find self proclaimed gurus telling you how it's mediocre in a video about how to get chicks by wearing suits and cologne. Don't be swayed, Sauvage is a great scent. It's strong without being overwhelming. It's spicy, citrusy, and a little smokey. Definitely a sophisticated, formal kind of scent. There's a reason it's a top pick for guys trying to impress their dates, it's because it's welcoming and confidence inspiring. A bit pricey but nothing too unreasonable. I'm on my second bottle after years because it doesn't take much. 2 sprays will do ya for the day.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="1571838"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=1571838#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent624082" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc624082" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Fogwalker"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/821659"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.821659.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Fogwalker" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Mauboussin/Mauboussin-Pour-Lui-in-Black-30138.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.30138.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Mauboussin Pour Lui in Black"title="Mauboussin Pour Lui in Black"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma624082ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd624082" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/821659">Fogwalker</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-08-25">08/25/15 10:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>OK, so after reading all the shameless scathing thrown @ Dior's latest offering, I had to make a visit to my local stockist to sample what all the fuss was(n't) about.<br />
I did the obligatory card-test first which came out as quite a strong, heavy, in-your-face blast of pepper with a hefty dose of aldehydes to boot. I then walked around the store before returning, to offer my neck and wrists a spray. I left the store and went about my business of doing some shopping.<br />
<br />
Two hours later, the smell remained heavy on me with very good projection.<br />
<br />
Three hours later, still no signs of letting go, this fragrance lost none of the original smell and followed me around like a stalker. Each time I turned my head, I could smell it wafting by.<br />
<br />
Some time later on my way home as I was stood waiting for the train doors to open, the lady aside me asked: "Is it you who smells nice?" I beckoned her towards my neck to sniff. Her reply: "Yes, it's you, that's beautiful, what is it?".<br />
An hour later buying a drink in a bar, the barman said: "You smell fresh, what are you wearing?"; before I had the chance to reply, another guy standing next to me said: "I wanted to ask the same question but was too shy".<br />
Not one but three compliments on Sauvage within as many hours. That's most definitely a first for me. I've never been complimented more than once in a week let alone a day regarding any fragrance I'm wearing.<br />
<br />
So, although my conclusion leaves me to say that this is by no means the best Dior fragrance I have had the pleasure to wear, I don't find it offensive in the slightest. Six hours later it's still smelling pretty strong on me, and, with (three) random strangers seemingly smitten by it, I think it will become a great seller for Dior.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="624082"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=624082#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent625515" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc625515" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="thehollowaytape"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/459558"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.459558.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="thehollowaytape" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma625515ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x0"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd625515" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/459558">thehollowaytape</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-08-30">08/30/15 00:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There is nothing wrong with this fragrance. You guys expecting every Dior release to be an iconic legend need to get off your high horse. Did Dior come steal your precious vintage Fahrenheit or Dior Homme Intense and replace it with Sauvage? No. Those other fragrances are still there. Go enjoy them and quit treating Fragrantica like reddit and bringing in the downvote brigade. I don't see anyone complaining about the other Dior men's fragrances that weren't ridiculously amazing (Jules, Higher, Dune).<br />
<br />
Anyway. This is a nice smelling, clean, fresh fragrance. Dior has a winner with this one, I can see it easily becoming a best seller. I know Dior believes this, too. I don't think they'd pony up for Depp if they didn't. It DOESN'T smell like Bleu de Chanel. (Which, by the way, everyone said was boring/sucked and is now one of the most recommended fragrances for guys who want just one.) It smells like citrus, spicy woods, and a touch of a musky character from the ambroxan. I put this on almost 8 hours ago and can still smell it well.<br />
<br />
Bottom line. Smell it for yourself. You might actually like it. If you don't... well hey, more for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="625515"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=625515#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="31861" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>
            </div>
</div>
</div><div class="tabs-panel" id="popular-negative-reviews"><div class="cell">
    <div class="strike-title"><span>Most Popular Negative Reviews</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
                            <div id="parent628585" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc628585" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Buysblind"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/52178"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.52178.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Buysblind" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Hermes/H24-65147.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.65147.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="H24"title="H24"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma628585ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd628585" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/52178">Buysblind</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-09-09">09/09/15 19:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Mediocre in every sense of the word. Sauvage opens with an abrasive, chemical interpretation of bergamot that's sweet and mildly pleasant. It transitions after about 10 or 15 minutes into a peppery dryer-sheet musk that is completely flat and linear and feels even more synthetic than the opening. I guess that's the ambroxan with some pepper added to it. Projection is solid and the longevity is around 6 to 8 hours. <br />
<br />
I disagree with anyone suggesting that Sauvage is of a better quality than the average designer fragrance on the market, at least as far as the ones in Sephora or Macy's are concerned. It's not. It smells cheaply made and totally insubstantial save for whatever overdose of synthetic fixatives keep it alive.   In comparison to Bleu de Chanel, Sauvage is vastly inferior. At least Bleu has some dimension and structure. It has development and solid, robust ingredients. Sauvage is absolutely anemic aside from its caustic, searing chemical edge which seems to provide its only strength. The only positive thing I have to say about it is that the smell itself is not bad--it's not unpleasant as a scent. But what's that really saying? Scent is subjective in that regard, so really anything can be "nice" or pleasant.   Cleaning products are pleasant too.  So are Glade Plug-Ins and those little trees people hang from their rearview mirror. Fabuloso smells great. And that's more or less what Sauvage has successfully replicated--your basic air freshener--vaguely representing all things common in men's cologne over the last 10 years. I've worn Sauvage 7 times, searching for any redeeming qualities it might possess and other than its inoffensiveness, and the fact that I kind of like the way ambroxan smells, I have found none. What's crazy to me is a lot of the people complaining over and over again about "another generic woody-amber" somehow give Sauvage a pass. Really?<br />
<br />
I'm not a fragrance snob or niche elitist or whatever other accusatory labels are getting thrown around to try and invalidate contrary opinions. My favorite release of the year was probably CK Reveal Men.  Yet again and again I hear the same old argument, "...but this fragrance is made for the average guy, it's not for the perfumistas and enthusiasts."  Well, no shit. And the average guy deserves better than this hollow, chemical dreck that wears as if it should cost $20 instead of $90, and can't hold a candle to its competition. Compliments? Who cares. Wear anything that leaves a solid trail and doesn't smell like you stepped out of a time warp or a horse stable and you WILL receive compliments. So you might as well pick up something decent while you're at it. Not this crap. Save your money. <br />
<br />
Thumbs down.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="628585"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=628585#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent628637" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc628637" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="alfarom"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/37900"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.37900.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="alfarom" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Serge-Lutens/Gris-Clair-593.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.593.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Gris Clair"title="Gris Clair"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma628637ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd628637" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/37900">alfarom</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-09-09">09/09/15 23:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I don't know where to start with Sauvage.<br />
<br />
For unknown reasons, I really wanted to like it. There's something about most Dior's mainstream masculines that's never *too banal* or *too cheap* and, on top of that, the association between the words Dior and Sauvage must have played some mental tricks on me and made me think about Roudnitska's classic Eau Sauvage. Ok, we all know this is not an Eau Sauvage flanker and as a new, massively advertised, delivery from Dior, I thought I couldn't have skipped it.<br />
<br />
For starters, this is not as bad as I expected. It's not even as bad as a rushed test might lead to think….but it's bad anyway in the end.<br />
<br />
I won't go through a proper note breakdown because there's really not much to mention here. The opening it's the most generic peppery-citrus combo you could expect from a whatever modern woody-citrus fragrance. Slightly aromatic, zingy and metallic.The first hour in, I was really this close to dismiss it but then a smooth mineral amber base (ambroxan) broke in together with vetiver and things slightly changed. The fragrance plays in the same league as other *depersonalizing*, post-disinfectant fragrances such as Bleu de Chanel, Guerlain's L'Homme Ideal and before these, D&amp;G Light Blue Pour Homme and L'Eau D'Issey but it takes the distance from the aforementioned perfumes by skipping that certain synth-y stickiness and / or loud volume that made all of them completely annoying to me. The Dior has a certain *raison d'être* provided by an elegant restraint and a class that is completely missing in most similar fragrances available on the market. It wears smooth and velvety with nice dark-ish facets in the base. It's extremely simple but, at least, they got right one of the two accords from which it is composed.<br />
<br />
Do I like it? Let's put it this way: It doesn't completely suck. In the end, while I surely believe Sauvage is by far the best fragrance in this post Bleu De Chanel-phase, I still wonder if we really needed a post Bleu De Chanel phase. It feels deprived of any emotional aspect but not in a creative kind of way. It's unemotional without that certain sparkle that makes the difference between the words *aseptic* and  *aloof*. It feels devoided. It's carb free, gluten free, peanut free, allergens free…it's too politically correct. Ok, it's well done but for me it's not enough and, in the end, I guess it's just another fragrance for people who actually don't like fragrances. <br />
<br />
Last but not least, I'm not the biggest fan of the Dior Homme saga but compared to this, they're completely on another level. Like completely.<br />
<br />
Rating: 5.5-6/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="628637"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=628637#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent850692" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Means I have co-worker wearing this almost daily and it is just so vile. What a synthetic mess, it smells just LOUD, screaming "I am here! I smell!" - it's not even trying to be aquatic, ocean-shower-fresh, green, woody or floral. Sauvage is just in-your-face aroma chemicals.<br />
Dior, you can and you have done a lot better than this!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="850692"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=850692#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent826599" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc826599" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Chiru"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1015703"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1015703.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Chiru" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Noir-Extreme-29675.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.29675.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Noir Extreme"title="Noir Extreme"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma826599ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x0"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd826599" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1015703">Chiru</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-05-27">05/27/17 14:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Hm... not really feeling this one guys. A frustrating fragrance in that it smells very synthetic, quite cosmetic and mall-like, and given the hype I was expecting a lot more. A very boring fragrance for the man with a perfect smile. It smells "perfect" but not in a good way. This is very much a modern male fragrance for modern males in the work setting, with no differentiating characteristics. Very machine-like and fake. It's hard to explain. I hope at least someone gets this reference... I know it's stupid, but it's pretty damn accurate:<br />
<br />
Remember that Spongebob episode where squidward wishes spongebob wasn't so goofy, and was more of a man's man agreeable neighbour? And spongebob becomes all rounded instead of square, is shiny and boring, but pleasant and agreeable, and also like every other typical guy? He just repeats "Hi, how are ya?" and seems fake? That's who I picture wearing this fragrance. Shallow, agreeable, boring yes-man guys in a suit at the office that smile at you and wave when you park your car up your driveway. About as multifaceted as a piece of paper and about as deep as a yogurt lid.<br />
<br />
It's just a generic, soapy department store kinda fragrance. Extremely safe, powdery, flowery, peppery and bright. I don't get the hype on this one. And I'm pretty open minded. I'm no snob who won't touch designer mainstream perfumes just because I think I'm some enlightened fellow who only sniffs interesting scents for interesting people. It just really is a boring scent, plain and simple. I know my review sounds bad, but it's not a -bad- scent per se. It's just... lacking anything to make it stand out. I'd pay maybe $40-50 for this scent. Maybe? But the asking price for this scent is absolutely insane for what it brings to the table. I have to echo what others are saying. It smells quite a bit like Bleu De Chanel, mixed with some peppery flowers and soapy powder. Perhaps people only like it because women seem to like it on men. It does have that fresh out of shower smell afterall. Thing is, every guy and their grandad wears this stuff, so for a perfume that everybody wears, it loses even more points towards purchasing it for me. How ironic that every guy wears a fragrance that just screams "every guy" in the first place. To each their own. <br />
<br />
I'm glad I tried this first and didn't spend the asking price for this perfume. A disappointment. Gosh, it really does just smell like hotel soap, lol. Really, this stuff smells like if you got a bar of  cheap Irish Spring soap and sprayed a bit of Bleu De Chanel on it. I mean I like it, please don't get me wrong, it's a very nice scent, and it does have good longevity, but at this price? And this boring? Nah. Want a typical soapy clean scent? Mugler Cologne is a lot cheaper to find and smells pretty decent. Want a subtle flowery work scent? Try Prada L'Homme which is incredible. Honestly there's just so many better options as far as soapy clean scents go that don't cost over $100 and have you smelling like every other guy. Try before you buy. All scents are subjective. You may love this. I'll repeat myself here, I would buy this scent at a discounted price. The drydown is pretty good, better than the opening for damn sure, but not great. If this was like $50 or lower, I'd absolutely get it. But no way in hell for the asking price right now.<br />
<br />
And another thing! How odd they called this "Sauvage". There's nothing "sauvage" about this in any stretch of the imagination. See that picture of Johhny Depp in the pictures section for this fragrance? Even he's making a "the fuck is this shit? sauvage? are you serious?" kinda face as he stares at the big white lettering of "Sauvage".<br />
<br />
Scent: 6/10, good drydown though.<br />
Silage: 7/10<br />
Longevity:8/10<br />
Personal Appreciation: 6/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="826599"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=826599#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent628673" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc628673" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="spoombung"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/54314"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.54314.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="spoombung" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Le-Labo/Oud-27-6329.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.6329.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Oud 27"title="Oud 27"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma628673ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd628673" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/54314">spoombung</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-09-10">09/10/15 03:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Air fresheners, deodorants, shower gels, shampoos, washing powder and fabric softeners have been creeping inexorably towards the world of designer perfume for years now and share many of the same aroma chemicals. Now it's the turn of some modern perfumes to step backwards and meet those household products on the centre ground. <br />
<br />
Sauvage is one such example. It is spectacularly ugly on first spray with a nauseating blast of laundry musk - akin to removing the lid from a bottle of fabric softener and poking your nose inside. This is then followed by the over- familiar and nebulous smell of air-freshener and supermarket body spray.<br />
<br />
It WILL register 'clean' for the men and women who associate laundry musk with clean floors, clean clothes and clean bathrooms but to many perfume fans this will also represent a disastrous lowering of standards from a well respected company that have brought us some superb products in the past.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31861"comment_id="628673"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-31861.html?ccid=628673#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="31861" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
            </div>
</div>
</div><div class="tabs-panel" id="search-reviews"><search-perfume-reviews :perfume_id="31861":random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]"></search-perfume-reviews></div></div><foundation-tabs></foundation-tabs></reviews-wrapper></div><perfume-shortcut-menu :perfume_id="31861" when-hidden="#toptop"></perfume-shortcut-menu><initialize-status-data></initialize-status-data><div class="cell small-12"><!-- 71161633/perfume_footer/perfume_footer --><div data-fuse="22384494437"></div></div></div>
